            None => None))))
 
 val
  removeFromAddAt as Chess/removeFromAddAt :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn sqSrc : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
       (fn sqDest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (case pieceAt2 pieces sqSrc.X sqSrc.Y of
           Some piece =>
            Some
             {1 = {Piece = piece.Piece, X = sqDest.X, Y = sqDest.Y}, 
               2 =
                removePSquare2
                 (removePSquare2 pieces sqSrc.X sqSrc.Y) sqDest.X
                 sqDest.Y} | None => pieces))))
 
 val rec
  rank_to_fenFrag as Chess/rank_to_fenFrag :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    FFI(Basis.int) ->
     FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.int) -> list(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn rank : FFI(Basis.int) =>
       (fn empty : FFI(Basis.int) =>
         (fn file : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (case (file == 8) of
             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
              (case (! (empty <= 0)) of
                FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                 Some {1 = FFI(Basis.intToString(empty)), 2 = None} | 
                 FFIC(Basis.False) => None) | 
              FFIC(Basis.False) =>
               (case pieceAt2 pieces file rank of
                 Some piece =>
                  Some
                   {1 =
                     (case (! (empty <= 0)) of
                       FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                        FFI(Basis.intToString(empty)) | 
                        FFIC(Basis.False) => ""), 
                     2 =
                      Some
                       {1 =
                         FFI(Basis.charToString)
                          (case piece.Piece of
                            BlackKing => #"k" | BlackQueen => #"q" | 
                             BlackRook => #"r" | 
                             BlackBishop => #"b" | 
                             BlackKnight => #"n" | 
                             BlackPawn => #"p" | WhiteKing => #"K" | 
                             WhiteQueen => #"Q" | WhiteRook => #"R" | 
                             WhiteBishop => #"B" | 
                             WhiteKnight => #"N" | WhitePawn => #"P"),
                                                                      
                         2 = rank_to_fenFrag pieces rank 0 (file + 1)}}
                                                                        |
                                                                        
                  None =>
                   rank_to_fenFrag pieces rank (empty + 1) (file + 1)))))))
 
 val rec
  $ra_unpoly as List/ra :
   list(FFI(Basis.string)) ->
    list(FFI(Basis.string)) -> list(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn ls : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
     (fn acc : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $ra_unpoly ls (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}))))
 
 val rec
  $rev'_unpoly as List/rev' :
   list(FFI(Basis.string)) ->
    list(FFI(Basis.string)) -> list(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn acc : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
     (fn ls : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $rev'_unpoly (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}) ls)))
 
 val rec
  $pieces_to_fen_aux as Chess/pieces_to_fen_aux :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    FFI(Basis.int) -> list(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn rank : FFI(Basis.int) =>
       (case (rank == 8) of
         FFIC(Basis.True) => None | 
          FFIC(Basis.False) =>
           $ra_unpoly
            ($rev'_unpoly None
              (Some {1 = "/", 2 = rank_to_fenFrag pieces rank 0 0}))
            ($pieces_to_fen_aux pieces (rank + 1)))))
 
 val
  sqStr as Chess/sqStr :
   {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} -> FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn sq : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
     (fileStr sq.X) ^ FFI(Basis.intToString(((7 - sq.Y) + 1))))
 
 val
  moveStr as Chess/moveStr :
   {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
     Prom : option(kind), 
     Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} ->
    FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn mov :
     {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
       Prom : option(kind), 
       Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} =>
     (sqStr mov.Src) ^
      (sqStr mov.Dest) ^
       (case mov.Prom of
         Some k =>
          (case k of
            King => "k" | Queen => "q" | Rook => "r" | 
             Bishop => "b" | Knight => "n" | Pawn => "p") | 
          None => ""))
 
 val
  $str_to_sq as Chess/str_to_sq :
   FFI(Basis.string) -> {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =
   (fn s : FFI(Basis.string) =>
     (let l : FFI(Basis.int) = (FFI(Basis.strlen(s))) in
      ((case (! (l <= 1)) of
         FFIC(Basis.True) =>
          (let snd : FFI(Basis.char) =
           (FFI(Basis.strsub(substring s 1 (l - 1), 0))) in
           ({X = fileToI FFI(Basis.strsub(s, 0)), 
              Y =
               (case FFI(Basis.isdigit(snd)) of
                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                  (case
                    FFI(Basis.stringToInt)
                     (FFI(Basis.charToString) snd) of
                    None => (- 1) | Some v => (7 - (v - 1))) | 
                  FFIC(Basis.False) => (- 1))})) | 
          FFIC(Basis.False) => {X = (- 1), Y = (- 1)}))))
 datatype sqPresence = Empty | Foe | Nvm
 
 val
  testSq as Chess/testSq :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player -> FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.int) -> sqPresence =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn x : FFI(Basis.int) =>
         (fn y : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (case validSq x y of
             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
              (case pieceAt2 pieces x y of
                Some piece =>
                 (case peq (piece_to_player piece.Piece) player of
                   FFIC(Basis.True) => Nvm | FFIC(Basis.False) => Foe)
                                                                       |
                                                                       
                 None => Empty) | FFIC(Basis.False) => Nvm)))))
 
 val
  pempty as Chess/pempty :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player -> FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn x : FFI(Basis.int) =>
         (fn y : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (case testSq pieces player x y of
             Empty => FFIC(Basis.True) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False))))))
 
 val
  pfoe as Chess/pfoe :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player -> FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn x : FFI(Basis.int) =>
         (fn y : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (case testSq pieces player x y of
             Foe => FFIC(Basis.True) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False))))))
 
 val
  pfoeOrSq as Chess/pfoeOrSq :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     FFI(Basis.int) ->
      FFI(Basis.int) ->
       option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
        FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn x : FFI(Basis.int) =>
         (fn y : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (fn sqq : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
             =>
             (case
               (case sqq of
                 Some sq =>
                  (case (x == sq.X) of
                    FFIC(Basis.True) => (y == sq.Y) | 
                     FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False)) | 
                  None => FFIC(Basis.False)) of
               FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                FFIC(Basis.False) => pfoe pieces player x y))))))
 
 val rec
  genSlide as Chess/genSlide :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      FFI(Basis.int) ->
       FFI(Basis.int) ->
        list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (fn dX : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (fn dY : FFI(Basis.int) =>
             (let testX : FFI(Basis.int) = ((src.X + dX)) in
              ((let testY : FFI(Basis.int) = ((src.Y + dY)) in
                ((case testSq pieces player testX testY of
                   Empty =>
                    Some
                     {1 = {X = testX, Y = testY}, 
                       2 =
                        genSlide pieces player {X = testX, Y = testY}
                         dX dY} | 
                    Foe =>
                     Some {1 = {X = testX, Y = testY}, 2 = None} | 
                    Nvm => None))))))))))
 
 val
  offTest as Chess/offTest :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      FFI(Basis.int) ->
       FFI(Basis.int) ->
        option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (fn dX : FFI(Basis.int) =>
           (fn dY : FFI(Basis.int) =>
             (let test : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =
              ({X = (src.X + dX), Y = (src.Y + dY)}) in
              ((case
                 (case testSq pieces player test.X test.Y of
                   Empty => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                    Foe => FFIC(Basis.True) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False))
                 of
                 FFIC(Basis.True) => Some test | 
                  FFIC(Basis.False) => None))))))))
 
 val rec
  removeNones_unpoly as Chess/removeNones :
   list(option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) ->
    list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn ls : list(option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =>
     (case ls of
       Some {1 = h, 2 = t} =>
        (case h of
          Some thing => Some {1 = thing, 2 = removeNones_unpoly t} | 
           None => removeNones_unpoly t) | None => None))
 
 val
  legalsKnight as Chess/legalsKnight :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         removeNones_unpoly
          (Some
            {1 = offTest pieces player src (- 1) (- 2), 
              2 =
               Some
                {1 = offTest pieces player src (- 1) 2, 
                  2 =
                   Some
                    {1 = offTest pieces player src 1 (- 2), 
                      2 =
                       Some
                        {1 = offTest pieces player src 1 2, 
                          2 =
                           Some
                            {1 =
                              offTest pieces player src (- 2) (- 1), 
                              2 =
                               Some
                                {1 =
                                  offTest pieces player src (- 2) 1, 
                                  2 =
                                   Some
                                    {1 =
                                      offTest pieces player src 2
                                       (- 1), 
                                      2 =
                                       Some
                                        {1 =
                                          offTest pieces player src 2
                                           1, 2 = None}}}}}}}}))))
 
 val rec
  $ra_unpoly as List/ra :
   list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn ls : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn acc : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $ra_unpoly ls (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}))))
 
 val rec
  $rev'_unpoly as List/rev' :
   list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn acc : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn ls : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $rev'_unpoly (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}) ls)))
 
 val
  legalsDiagonals as Chess/legalsDiagonals :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         $ra_unpoly
          ($rev'_unpoly None
            ($ra_unpoly
              ($rev'_unpoly None
                (genSlide pieces player src (- 1) (- 1)))
              (genSlide pieces player src 1 (- 1))))
          ($ra_unpoly
            ($rev'_unpoly None (genSlide pieces player src (- 1) 1))
            (genSlide pieces player src 1 1)))))
 
 val
  legalsOrtho as Chess/legalsOrtho :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         $ra_unpoly
          ($rev'_unpoly None
            ($ra_unpoly
              ($rev'_unpoly None (genSlide pieces player src 0 (- 1)))
              (genSlide pieces player src 0 1)))
          ($ra_unpoly
            ($rev'_unpoly None (genSlide pieces player src (- 1) 0))
            (genSlide pieces player src 1 0)))))
 
 val
  legalsSlide as Chess/legalsSlide :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    player ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
      list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn player : player =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         $ra_unpoly
          ($rev'_unpoly None (legalsDiagonals pieces player src))
          (legalsOrtho pieces player src))))
 
 val rec
  hasDest as Chess/hasDest :
   list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn ls : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn sq : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
       (case ls of
         Some {1 = h, 2 = t} =>
          (case
            (case (h.X == sq.X) of
              FFIC(Basis.True) => (h.Y == sq.Y) | 
               FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False)) of
            FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
             FFIC(Basis.False) => hasDest t sq) | 
          None => FFIC(Basis.False))))
 
 val rec
  hasDestOneOf as Chess/hasDestOneOf :
   list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) -> FFI(Basis.bool)
   =
   (fn ls : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn lssq : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
       (case lssq of
         Some {1 = h, 2 = t} =>
          (case hasDest ls h of
            FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
             FFIC(Basis.False) => hasDestOneOf ls t) | 
          None => FFIC(Basis.False))))
 
 val
  legalsForPiece as Chess/legalsForPiece :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    {Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
     list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn piece :
       {Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
       (case piece_to_kind piece.Piece of
         Pawn =>
          (let player : player = (piece_to_player piece.Piece) in
           ((case player of
              White =>
               $ra_unpoly
                ($rev'_unpoly None
                  ($ra_unpoly
                    ($rev'_unpoly None
                      (case
                        (case
                          (case (piece.Y == 6) of
                            FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                             pempty state.Pieces player piece.X
                              (piece.Y - 1) | 
                             FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))
                          of
                          FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                           pempty state.Pieces player piece.X
                            (piece.Y - 2) | 
                           FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                        FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                         Some
                          {1 = {X = piece.X, Y = (piece.Y - 2)}, 
                            2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                    (case
                      pempty state.Pieces player piece.X
                       (piece.Y - 1) of
                      FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                       Some
                        {1 = {X = piece.X, Y = (piece.Y - 1)}, 
                          2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None)))
                ($ra_unpoly
                  ($rev'_unpoly None
                    (case
                      pfoeOrSq state.Pieces player (piece.X - 1)
                       (piece.Y - 1) state.EnPassant of
                      FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                       Some
                        {1 = {X = (piece.X - 1), Y = (piece.Y - 1)}, 
                          2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                  (case
                    pfoeOrSq state.Pieces player (piece.X + 1)
                     (piece.Y - 1) state.EnPassant of
                    FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                     Some
                      {1 = {X = (piece.X + 1), Y = (piece.Y - 1)}, 
                        2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None)) | 
               Black =>
                $ra_unpoly
                 ($rev'_unpoly None
                   ($ra_unpoly
                     ($rev'_unpoly None
                       (case
                         (case
                           (case (piece.Y == 1) of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                              pempty state.Pieces player piece.X
                               (piece.Y + 1) | 
                              FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))
                           of
                           FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                            pempty state.Pieces player piece.X
                             (piece.Y + 2) | 
                            FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))
                         of
                         FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                          Some
                           {1 = {X = piece.X, Y = (piece.Y + 2)}, 
                             2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                     (case
                       pempty state.Pieces player piece.X
                        (piece.Y + 1) of
                       FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                        Some
                         {1 = {X = piece.X, Y = (piece.Y + 1)}, 
                           2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None)))
                 ($ra_unpoly
                   ($rev'_unpoly None
                     (case
                       pfoeOrSq state.Pieces player (piece.X - 1)
                        (piece.Y + 1) state.EnPassant of
                       FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                        Some
                         {1 = {X = (piece.X - 1), Y = (piece.Y + 1)}, 
                           2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                   (case
                     pfoeOrSq state.Pieces player (piece.X + 1)
                      (piece.Y + 1) state.EnPassant of
                     FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                      Some
                       {1 = {X = (piece.X + 1), Y = (piece.Y + 1)}, 
                         2 = None} | FFIC(Basis.False) => None))))) | 
          Bishop =>
           legalsDiagonals state.Pieces (piece_to_player piece.Piece)
            {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} | 
          Rook =>
           legalsOrtho state.Pieces (piece_to_player piece.Piece)
            {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} | 
          Queen =>
           legalsSlide state.Pieces (piece_to_player piece.Piece)
            {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} | 
          Knight =>
           legalsKnight state.Pieces (piece_to_player piece.Piece)
            {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} | 
          King =>
           (let player : player = (piece_to_player piece.Piece) in
            (removeNones_unpoly
              (Some
                {1 =
                  offTest state.Pieces player
                   {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} (- 1) 1, 
                  2 =
                   Some
                    {1 =
                      offTest state.Pieces player
                       {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} (- 1) 0, 
                      2 =
                       Some
                        {1 =
                          offTest state.Pieces player
                           {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} (- 1) (- 1), 
                          2 =
                           Some
                            {1 =
                              offTest state.Pieces player
                               {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} 1 1, 
                              2 =
                               Some
                                {1 =
                                  offTest state.Pieces player
                                   {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} 1 0, 
                                  2 =
                                   Some
                                    {1 =
                                      offTest state.Pieces player
                                       {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y} 1
                                       (- 1), 
                                      2 =
                                       Some
                                        {1 =
                                          offTest state.Pieces player
                                           {X = piece.X, Y = piece.Y}
                                           0 1, 
                                          2 =
                                           Some
                                            {1 =
                                              offTest state.Pieces
                                               player
                                               {X = piece.X, 
                                                 Y = piece.Y} 0 (- 1),
                                                                      
                                              2 =
                                               Some
                                                {1 =
                                                  (case
                                                    (case player of
                                                      White =>
                                                       state.WK | 
                                                       Black =>
                                                        state.BK) of
                                                    FFIC(Basis.True)
                                                     =>
                                                     offTest
                                                      state.Pieces
                                                      player
                                                      {X = piece.X, 
                                                        Y = piece.Y}
                                                      2 0 | 
                                                     FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                      => None), 
                                                  2 =
                                                   Some
                                                    {1 =
                                                      (case
                                                        (case player
                                                          of
                                                          White =>
                                                           state.WQ | 
                                                           Black =>
                                                            state.BQ)
                                                        of
                                                        FFIC(Basis.True)
                                                         =>
                                                         offTest
                                                          state.Pieces
                                                          player
                                                          {X =
                                                            piece.X, 
                                                            Y =
                                                             piece.Y}
                                                          (- 2) 0 | 
                                                         FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                          => None), 
                                                      2 = None}}}}}}}}}}))))))
 
 val rec
  $rev'_unpoly as List/rev' :
   list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) ->
    list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) ->
     list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =
   (fn acc : list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =>
     (fn ls : list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $rev'_unpoly (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}) ls)))
 
 val rec
  $rev'_unpoly as List/rev' :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn acc :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn ls :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
       =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $rev'_unpoly (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}) ls)))
 
 val rec
  $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly as List/foldl' :
   list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) ->
     list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn acc : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn ls : list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly
            ($ra_unpoly ($rev'_unpoly None x) acc) ls)))
 
 val rec
  $mp'_unpoly_unpoly as List/mp' :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) ->
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
      list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn acc : list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}))
       =>
       (fn ls :
         list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
         =>
         (case ls of
           None => $rev'_unpoly None acc | 
            Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
             $mp'_unpoly_unpoly state
              (Some {1 = legalsForPiece state x, 2 = acc}) ls))))
 
 val rec
  $fil_unpoly as List/fil :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn acc :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
       =>
       (fn ls :
         list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
         =>
         (case ls of
           None => $rev'_unpoly None acc | 
            Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
             $fil_unpoly state
              (case peq state.Player (piece_to_player x.Piece) of
                FFIC(Basis.True) => Some {1 = x, 2 = acc} | 
                 FFIC(Basis.False) => acc) ls))))
 
 val
  allLegals as Chess/allLegals :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly None
      ($mp'_unpoly_unpoly state None
        ($fil_unpoly state None state.Pieces)))
 
 val
  requiresPromotion as Chess/requiresPromotion :
   {Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
    FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn piece :
     {Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
     (fn destY : FFI(Basis.int) =>
       (case piece_to_kind piece.Piece of
         Pawn =>
          (case piece_to_player piece.Piece of
            White => (destY == 0) | Black => (destY == 7)) | 
          _ => FFIC(Basis.False))))
 
 val
  isKingMove as Chess/isKingMove :
   player ->
    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn player : player =>
     (fn pieces :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
       =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (case pieceAt2 pieces src.X src.Y of
           None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
            Some p =>
             (case peq (piece_to_player p.Piece) player of
               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                  King => FFIC(Basis.True) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False))
                                                                     |
                                                                     
                FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))))))
 
 val
  isRookQMove as Chess/isRookQMove :
   player ->
    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn player : player =>
     (fn pieces :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
       =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (case pieceAt2 pieces src.X src.Y of
           None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
            Some p =>
             (case peq (piece_to_player p.Piece) player of
               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                  Rook => (p.X < 4) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False)) | 
                FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))))))
 
 val
  isRookKMove as Chess/isRookKMove :
   player ->
    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} -> FFI(Basis.bool) =
   (fn player : player =>
     (fn pieces :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
       =>
       (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (case pieceAt2 pieces src.X src.Y of
           None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
            Some p =>
             (case peq (piece_to_player p.Piece) player of
               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                  Rook => (! (p.X <= 4)) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False)) | 
                FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))))))
 
 val
  isCastle as Chess/isCastle :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} ->
     {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} -> option(castle) =
   (fn pieces :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (fn src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
       (fn dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} =>
         (case pieceAt2 pieces src.X src.Y of
           None => None | 
            Some p =>
             (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
               King =>
                (case
                  (!
                    ((FFI(Basis.floatFromInt(dest.X)) -
                       FFI(Basis.floatFromInt(src.X))) <= 1)) of
                  FFIC(Basis.True) => Some Kingside | 
                   FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                    (case
                      ((FFI(Basis.floatFromInt(dest.X)) -
                         FFI(Basis.floatFromInt(src.X))) < (- 1)) of
                      FFIC(Basis.True) => Some Queenside | 
                       FFIC(Basis.False) => None)) | _ => None)))))
 
 val
  fen_to_state as Helloworld/fen_to_state :
   FFI(Basis.string) ->
    {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
      EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
      FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
      Pieces :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
      Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =
   (fn s : FFI(Basis.string) => $fen_to_pieces_aux s 0 0 None)
 
 val rec
  removeNones_unpoly as Chess/removeNones :
   list(option(FFI(Basis.string))) -> list(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn ls : list(option(FFI(Basis.string))) =>
     (case ls of
       Some {1 = h, 2 = t} =>
        (case h of
          Some thing => Some {1 = thing, 2 = removeNones_unpoly t} | 
           None => removeNones_unpoly t) | None => None))
 
 val rec
  $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly as List/foldl' :
   FFI(Basis.string) -> list(FFI(Basis.string)) -> FFI(Basis.string)
   =
   (fn acc : FFI(Basis.string) =>
     (fn ls : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} => $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly (x ^ acc) ls)))
 
 val
  state_to_fen as Helloworld/state_to_fen :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly ""
      ($rev'_unpoly None
        ($ra_unpoly
          ($rev'_unpoly None
            ($ra_unpoly
              ($rev'_unpoly None (rank_to_fenFrag state.Pieces 0 0 0))
              ($pieces_to_fen_aux state.Pieces 1)))
          (Some
            {1 = " ", 
              2 =
               Some
                {1 =
                  (case state.Player of White => "w" | Black => "b"), 
                  2 =
                   $ra_unpoly
                    ($rev'_unpoly None
                      (Some
                        {1 = " ", 
                          2 =
                           (case
                             (case
                               (case
                                 (case state.WK of
                                   FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                    FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                                    FFIC(Basis.False) => state.WQ) of
                                 FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True)
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                                  FFIC(Basis.False) => state.BK) of
                               FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                                FFIC(Basis.False) => state.BQ) of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                              removeNones_unpoly
                               (Some
                                 {1 =
                                   (case state.WK of
                                     FFIC(Basis.True) => Some "K" | 
                                      FFIC(Basis.False) => None), 
                                   2 =
                                    Some
                                     {1 =
                                       (case state.WQ of
                                         FFIC(Basis.True) => Some "Q"
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                                          FFIC(Basis.False) => None), 
                                       2 =
                                        Some
                                         {1 =
                                           (case state.BK of
                                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                              Some "k" | 
                                              FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                               None), 
                                           2 =
                                            Some
                                             {1 =
                                               (case state.BQ of
                                                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                                  Some "q" | 
                                                  FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                   => None), 2 = None}}}})
                                                                           |
                                                                           
                              FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                               Some {1 = "-", 2 = None})}))
                    ($ra_unpoly
                      ($rev'_unpoly None
                        (Some
                          {1 = " ", 
                            2 =
                             (case state.EnPassant of
                               None => Some {1 = "-", 2 = None} | 
                                Some sq =>
                                 Some {1 = sqStr sq, 2 = None})}))
                      (Some
                        {1 = " ", 
                          2 =
                           Some
                            {1 =
                              FFI(Basis.intToString(state.HalfMove)), 
                              2 =
                               Some
                                {1 = " ", 
                                  2 =
                                   Some
                                    {1 =
                                      FFI(Basis.intToString(state.FullMove)),
                                                                             
                                      2 = None}}}}))}}))))
 
 val
  doMove as Helloworld/doMove :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
      Prom : option(kind), 
      Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} ->
     option({BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
              EnPassant :
               option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
              FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
              Pieces :
               list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                      Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
              WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn move :
       {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
         Prom : option(kind), 
         Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} =>
       (case
         (case pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Src.X move.Src.Y of
           Some piece =>
            (case peq (piece_to_player piece.Piece) state.Player of
              FFIC(Basis.True) =>
               (case hasDest (legalsForPiece state piece) move.Dest
                 of
                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                  (case move.Prom of
                    None =>
                     (case requiresPromotion piece move.Dest.Y of
                       FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                        FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.True)) | 
                     Some k =>
                      (case requiresPromotion piece move.Dest.Y of
                        FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                         (case k of
                           Queen => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                            Rook => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                            Bishop => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                            Knight => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                            _ => FFIC(Basis.False)) | 
                         FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))) | 
                  FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False)) | 
               FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False)) | 
            None => FFIC(Basis.False)) of
         FFIC(Basis.True) =>
          (let requiresEnPassant : FFI(Basis.bool) =
           ((case pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Src.X move.Src.Y of
              None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
               Some p =>
                (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                  Pawn =>
                   (FFI(Basis.abs((FFI(Basis.floatFromInt(move.Src.Y))
                                    -
                                    FFI(Basis.floatFromInt(move.Dest.Y)))))
                     == 2) | _ => FFIC(Basis.False)))) in
           ((let piecesnew :
             list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                    Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
             (removeFromAddAt state.Pieces move.Src move.Dest) in
             ((let castled : option(castle) =
               (isCastle state.Pieces move.Src move.Dest) in
               ((let resetCounter : FFI(Basis.bool) =
                 ((case pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Dest.X move.Dest.Y
                    of
                    None =>
                     (case
                       pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Src.X move.Dest.Y
                       of
                       None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                        Some p =>
                         (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                           Pawn => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                            _ => FFIC(Basis.False))) | 
                     Some _ => FFIC(Basis.True))) in
                 ((let piecesnew2 :
                   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                          Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
                   ((case castled of
                      Some Kingside =>
                       removeFromAddAt piecesnew
                        {X = 7, Y = move.Src.Y}
                        {X = 5, Y = move.Src.Y} | 
                       Some Queenside =>
                        removeFromAddAt piecesnew
                         {X = 0, Y = move.Src.Y}
                         {X = 3, Y = move.Src.Y} | None => piecesnew))
                   in
                   ((let piecesnew3 :
                     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                            Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
                     ((case
                        (case state.EnPassant of
                          None => None | 
                           Some sq =>
                            (case
                              (case (move.Dest.X == sq.X) of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                 (move.Dest.Y == sq.Y) | 
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                  FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                              FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                               (case
                                 pieceAt2 piecesnew2 move.Dest.X
                                  move.Dest.Y of
                                 None => None | 
                                  Some p =>
                                   (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                                     Pawn =>
                                      Some
                                       (let back : FFI(Basis.int) =
                                        ((case state.Player of
                                           White => 1 | 
                                            Black => (- 1))) in
                                        ({X = sq.X, Y = (sq.Y + back)}))
                                                                         |
                                                                         
                                      _ => None)) | 
                               FFIC(Basis.False) => None)) of
                        None => piecesnew2 | 
                         Some sq =>
                          removePSquare2 piecesnew2 sq.X sq.Y)) in
                     ((let newState :
                       {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
                         EnPassant :
                          option({X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                                   Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
                         FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
                         HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
                         Pieces :
                          list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                                 Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
                         Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), 
                         WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =
                       ({BK =
                          (case
                            (case state.BK of
                              FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                               peq Black state.Player | 
                               FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.False))
                            of
                            FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                             (case
                               (case
                                 isKingMove Black state.Pieces
                                  move.Src of
                                 FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True)
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                                  FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                   isRookKMove Black state.Pieces
                                    move.Src) of
                               FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                                     |
                                                                     
                                FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.True))
                                                                       |
                                                                       
                             FFIC(Basis.False) => state.BK), 
                          BQ =
                           (case
                             (case state.BQ of
                               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                peq Black state.Player | 
                                FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                 FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                              (case
                                (case
                                  isKingMove Black state.Pieces
                                   move.Src of
                                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                   FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                                   FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                    isRookQMove Black state.Pieces
                                     move.Src) of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                  FFIC(Basis.True)) | 
                              FFIC(Basis.False) => state.BQ), 
                          EnPassant =
                           (case requiresEnPassant of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                              (case state.Player of
                                White =>
                                 Some
                                  {X = move.Dest.X, 
                                    Y = (move.Dest.Y + 1)} | 
                                 Black =>
                                  Some
                                   {X = move.Dest.X, 
                                     Y = (move.Dest.Y - 1)}) | 
                              FFIC(Basis.False) => None), 
                          FullMove =
                           (case peq state.Player Black of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) => (state.FullMove + 1)
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                              FFIC(Basis.False) => state.FullMove), 
                          HalfMove =
                           (case resetCounter of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) => 0 | 
                              FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                               (state.HalfMove + 1)), 
                          Pieces =
                           (case move.Prom of
                             None => piecesnew3 | 
                              Some k =>
                               Some
                                {1 =
                                  {Piece =
                                    (case state.Player of
                                      White =>
                                       (case k of
                                         King => WhiteKing | 
                                          Queen => WhiteQueen | 
                                          Rook => WhiteRook | 
                                          Bishop => WhiteBishop | 
                                          Knight => WhiteKnight | 
                                          Pawn => WhitePawn) | 
                                       Black =>
                                        (case k of
                                          King => BlackKing | 
                                           Queen => BlackQueen | 
                                           Rook => BlackRook | 
                                           Bishop => BlackBishop | 
                                           Knight => BlackKnight | 
                                           Pawn => BlackPawn)), 
                                    X = move.Dest.X, Y = move.Dest.Y},
                                                                      
                                  2 =
                                   removePSquare2 piecesnew3
                                    move.Dest.X move.Dest.Y}), 
                          Player =
                           (case state.Player of
                             White => Black | Black => White), 
                          WK =
                           (case
                             (case state.WK of
                               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                peq White state.Player | 
                                FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                 FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                              (case
                                (case
                                  isKingMove White state.Pieces
                                   move.Src of
                                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                   FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                                   FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                    isRookKMove White state.Pieces
                                     move.Src) of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                  FFIC(Basis.True)) | 
                              FFIC(Basis.False) => state.WK), 
                          WQ =
                           (case
                             (case state.WQ of
                               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                peq White state.Player | 
                                FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                 FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                             FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                              (case
                                (case
                                  isKingMove White state.Pieces
                                   move.Src of
                                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                   FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                                   FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                    isRookQMove White state.Pieces
                                     move.Src) of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                  FFIC(Basis.True)) | 
                              FFIC(Basis.False) => state.WQ)}) in
                       ((case
                          (case
                            pieceAtKP newState.Pieces King
                             (case newState.Player of
                               White => Black | Black => White) of
                            None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                             Some prec =>
                              (let moves :
                               list({X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                                      Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
                               (allLegals newState) in
                               ((case
                                  (case castled of
                                    None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                                     Some Kingside =>
                                      hasDestOneOf moves
                                       (Some
                                         {1 = {X = 4, Y = move.Src.Y},
                                                                      
                                           2 =
                                            Some
                                             {1 =
                                               {X = 5, Y = move.Src.Y},
                                                                       
                                               2 =
                                                Some
                                                 {1 =
                                                   {X = 6, 
                                                     Y = move.Src.Y}, 
                                                   2 = None}}}) | 
                                     Some Queenside =>
                                      hasDestOneOf moves
                                       (Some
                                         {1 = {X = 4, Y = move.Src.Y},
                                                                      
                                           2 =
                                            Some
                                             {1 =
                                               {X = 3, Y = move.Src.Y},
                                                                       
                                               2 =
                                                Some
                                                 {1 =
                                                   {X = 2, 
                                                     Y = move.Src.Y}, 
                                                   2 = None}}})) of
                                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                   FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                                   FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                    hasDest moves
                                     {X = prec.X, Y = prec.Y})))) of
                          FFIC(Basis.True) => None | 
                           FFIC(Basis.False) => Some newState)))))))))))))))
                                                                             |
                                                                             
          FFIC(Basis.False) => None)))
 
 val rec
  $mp'_unpoly_unpoly as List/mp' :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) ->
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
      list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})) =
   (fn nextstate :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn acc : list(list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}))
       =>
       (fn ls :
         list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
         =>
         (case ls of
           None => $rev'_unpoly None acc | 
            Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
             $mp'_unpoly_unpoly nextstate
              (Some
                {1 =
                  (case piece_to_kind x.Piece of
                    Pawn =>
                     (let player : player = (piece_to_player x.Piece)
                      in
                      ((case player of
                         White =>
                          $ra_unpoly
                           ($rev'_unpoly None
                             ($ra_unpoly
                               ($rev'_unpoly None
                                 (case
                                   (case
                                     (case (x.Y == 6) of
                                       FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                        pempty nextstate.Pieces
                                         player x.X (x.Y - 1) | 
                                        FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                         FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                                     FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                      pempty nextstate.Pieces player
                                       x.X (x.Y - 2) | 
                                      FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                       FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                                   FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                    Some
                                     {1 = {X = x.X, Y = (x.Y - 2)}, 
                                       2 = None} | 
                                    FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                               (case
                                 pempty nextstate.Pieces player x.X
                                  (x.Y - 1) of
                                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                  Some
                                   {1 = {X = x.X, Y = (x.Y - 1)}, 
                                     2 = None} | 
                                  FFIC(Basis.False) => None)))
                           ($ra_unpoly
                             ($rev'_unpoly None
                               (case
                                 pfoe nextstate.Pieces player
                                  (x.X - 1) (x.Y - 1) of
                                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                  Some
                                   {1 =
                                     {X = (x.X - 1), Y = (x.Y - 1)}, 
                                     2 = None} | 
                                  FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                             (case
                               pfoe nextstate.Pieces player (x.X + 1)
                                (x.Y - 1) of
                               FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                Some
                                 {1 = {X = (x.X + 1), Y = (x.Y - 1)}, 
                                   2 = None} | 
                                FFIC(Basis.False) => None)) | 
                          Black =>
                           $ra_unpoly
                            ($rev'_unpoly None
                              ($ra_unpoly
                                ($rev'_unpoly None
                                  (case
                                    (case
                                      (case (x.Y == 1) of
                                        FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                         pempty nextstate.Pieces
                                          player x.X (x.Y + 1) | 
                                         FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                          FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                                      FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                       pempty nextstate.Pieces player
                                        x.X (x.Y + 2) | 
                                       FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                        FFIC(Basis.False)) of
                                    FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                     Some
                                      {1 = {X = x.X, Y = (x.Y + 2)}, 
                                        2 = None} | 
                                     FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                                (case
                                  pempty nextstate.Pieces player x.X
                                   (x.Y + 1) of
                                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                   Some
                                    {1 = {X = x.X, Y = (x.Y + 1)}, 
                                      2 = None} | 
                                   FFIC(Basis.False) => None)))
                            ($ra_unpoly
                              ($rev'_unpoly None
                                (case
                                  pfoe nextstate.Pieces player
                                   (x.X - 1) (x.Y + 1) of
                                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                   Some
                                    {1 =
                                      {X = (x.X - 1), Y = (x.Y + 1)}, 
                                      2 = None} | 
                                   FFIC(Basis.False) => None))
                              (case
                                pfoe nextstate.Pieces player
                                 (x.X + 1) (x.Y + 1) of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                 Some
                                  {1 = {X = (x.X + 1), Y = (x.Y + 1)},
                                                                      
                                    2 = None} | 
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) => None))))) | 
                     Bishop =>
                      legalsDiagonals nextstate.Pieces
                       (piece_to_player x.Piece) {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} | 
                     Rook =>
                      legalsOrtho nextstate.Pieces
                       (piece_to_player x.Piece) {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} | 
                     Queen =>
                      legalsSlide nextstate.Pieces
                       (piece_to_player x.Piece) {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} | 
                     Knight =>
                      legalsKnight nextstate.Pieces
                       (piece_to_player x.Piece) {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} | 
                     King =>
                      (let player : player =
                       (piece_to_player x.Piece) in
                       (removeNones_unpoly
                         (Some
                           {1 =
                             offTest nextstate.Pieces player
                              {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} (- 1) 1, 
                             2 =
                              Some
                               {1 =
                                 offTest nextstate.Pieces player
                                  {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} (- 1) 0, 
                                 2 =
                                  Some
                                   {1 =
                                     offTest nextstate.Pieces player
                                      {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} (- 1) (- 1), 
                                     2 =
                                      Some
                                       {1 =
                                         offTest nextstate.Pieces
                                          player {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} 1
                                          1, 
                                         2 =
                                          Some
                                           {1 =
                                             offTest nextstate.Pieces
                                              player
                                              {X = x.X, Y = x.Y} 1 0, 
                                             2 =
                                              Some
                                               {1 =
                                                 offTest
                                                  nextstate.Pieces
                                                  player
                                                  {X = x.X, Y = x.Y}
                                                  1 (- 1), 
                                                 2 =
                                                  Some
                                                   {1 =
                                                     offTest
                                                      nextstate.Pieces
                                                      player
                                                      {X = x.X, 
                                                        Y = x.Y} 0 1, 
                                                     2 =
                                                      Some
                                                       {1 =
                                                         offTest
                                                          nextstate.Pieces
                                                          player
                                                          {X = x.X, 
                                                            Y = x.Y}
                                                          0 (- 1), 
                                                         2 = None}}}}}}}})))),
                                                                              
                  2 = acc}) ls))))
 
 val rec
  $fil_unpoly as List/fil :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =
   (fn nextstate :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn acc :
       list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
       =>
       (fn ls :
         list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)})
         =>
         (case ls of
           None => $rev'_unpoly None acc | 
            Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
             $fil_unpoly nextstate
              (case
                peq
                 (case nextstate.Player of
                   White => Black | Black => White)
                 (piece_to_player x.Piece) of
                FFIC(Basis.True) => Some {1 = x, 2 = acc} | 
                 FFIC(Basis.False) => acc) ls))))
 
 val
  moveToAlgebraicClean as Helloworld/moveToAlgebraicClean :
   {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
     EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
     Pieces :
      list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
     Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} ->
    {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
      Prom : option(kind), 
      Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} ->
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
      -> FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn state :
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
     =>
     (fn move :
       {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
         Prom : option(kind), 
         Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} =>
       (fn nextstate :
         {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
           EnPassant :
            option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
           FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
           Pieces :
            list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                   Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
           WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =>
         (let regularX : FFI(Basis.bool) =
          ((case
             {1 = pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Dest.X move.Dest.Y, 
               2 = pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Src.X move.Src.Y} of
             {1 = Some p, 2 = Some p'} =>
              (case
                peq (piece_to_player p.Piece)
                 (piece_to_player p'.Piece) of
                FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                 FFIC(Basis.False) => FFIC(Basis.True)) | 
              {1 = _, 2 = _} => FFIC(Basis.False))) in
          ((let isCheck : FFI(Basis.bool) =
            ((case pieceAtKP nextstate.Pieces King nextstate.Player
               of
               None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                Some krec =>
                 hasDest
                  ($foldl'_unpoly_unpoly None
                    ($mp'_unpoly_unpoly nextstate None
                      ($fil_unpoly nextstate None nextstate.Pieces)))
                  {X = krec.X, Y = krec.Y})) in
            ((let anyLegals : FFI(Basis.bool) =
              ((case allLegals nextstate of
                 None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                  Some {1 = _, 2 = _} => FFIC(Basis.True))) in
              ((let checkSuffix : FFI(Basis.string) =
                ((case isCheck of
                   FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                    (case anyLegals of
                      FFIC(Basis.True) => "+" | 
                       FFIC(Basis.False) => "#") | 
                    FFIC(Basis.False) => "")) in
                ((case pieceAt2 state.Pieces move.Src.X move.Src.Y of
                   None => "" | 
                    Some p =>
                     (case piece_to_kind p.Piece of
                       Pawn =>
                        (case
                          (case state.EnPassant of
                            None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                             Some sq' =>
                              (case (sq'.X == move.Dest.X) of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                 (sq'.Y == move.Dest.Y) | 
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                  FFIC(Basis.False))) of
                          FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                           (fileStr move.Src.X) ^
                            "x" ^
                             (sqStr move.Dest) ^ "e.p." ^ checkSuffix
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                           FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                            (case regularX of
                              FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                               (fileStr move.Src.X) ^
                                "x" ^ (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                               FFIC(Basis.False) =>
                                (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix)) | 
                        Knight =>
                         "N" ^
                          (case regularX of
                            FFIC(Basis.True) => "x" | 
                             FFIC(Basis.False) => "") ^
                           (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix | 
                        Bishop =>
                         "B" ^
                          (case regularX of
