                            FFIC(Basis.True) => "x" | 
                             FFIC(Basis.False) => "") ^
                           (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix | 
                        Rook =>
                         "R" ^
                          (case regularX of
                            FFIC(Basis.True) => "x" | 
                             FFIC(Basis.False) => "") ^
                           (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix | 
                        Queen =>
                         "Q" ^
                          (case regularX of
                            FFIC(Basis.True) => "x" | 
                             FFIC(Basis.False) => "") ^
                           (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix | 
                        King =>
                         (case
                           isCastle state.Pieces move.Src move.Dest
                           of
                           Some Kingside => "O-O" ^ checkSuffix | 
                            Some Queenside => "O-O-O" ^ checkSuffix | 
                            None =>
                             "K" ^
                              (case regularX of
                                FFIC(Basis.True) => "x" | 
                                 FFIC(Basis.False) => "") ^
                               (sqStr move.Dest) ^ checkSuffix) | 
                        _ => moveStr move)))))))))))))
 
 val
  str_to_move as Helloworld/str_to_move :
   FFI(Basis.string) ->
    {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
      Prom : option(kind), 
      Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
   (fn str : FFI(Basis.string) =>
     (let len : FFI(Basis.int) = (FFI(Basis.strlen(str))) in
      ({Dest = $str_to_sq (substring str 2 (len - 2)), 
         Prom =
          (case substring str 4 (len - 4) of
            "k" => Some King | "q" => Some Queen | "r" => Some Rook | 
             "b" => Some Bishop | "n" => Some Knight | 
             "p" => Some Pawn | _ => None), Src = $str_to_sq str})))
 style move-clickable

    Position of
     {Highlight : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       Id : FFI(Basis.int), 
       State :
        {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
          EnPassant :
           option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
          FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
          Pieces :
           list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                  Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
          WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}}

      2 : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}, 3 : option(kind)}
                                                                      |
                                                                      
    SHighlight of {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)} | SBack | 
    SForward | SPosition of FFI(Basis.int)

 (* SQL table uw_Helloworld_Room_t :

 val rec
  urlify_list as  :
   list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn x :
     list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (case x of
       None => "Nil" | 
        Some a =>
         "Cons/" ^
          (case a.1.Piece of
            WhiteKing => "WhiteKing" | WhiteQueen => "WhiteQueen" | 
             WhiteRook => "WhiteRook" | 
             WhiteBishop => "WhiteBishop" | 
             WhiteKnight => "WhiteKnight" | 
             WhitePawn => "WhitePawn" | BlackKing => "BlackKing" | 
             BlackQueen => "BlackQueen" | BlackRook => "BlackRook" | 
             BlackBishop => "BlackBishop" | 
             BlackKnight => "BlackKnight" | BlackPawn => "BlackPawn")
           ^
           "/" ^
            FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.1.X)) ^
             "/" ^
              FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.1.Y)) ^ "/" ^ urlify_list a.2))
 
 val rec
  urlify_list as  :
   list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
    FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn x : list({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}) =>
     (case x of
       None => "Nil" | 
        Some a =>
         "Cons/" ^
          FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.1.X)) ^
           "/" ^ FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.1.Y)) ^ "/" ^ urlify_list a.2))
 
 val
  send as Helloworld/Room/send :
   FFI(Basis.int) -> boardmsg -> {} -> {} =
   (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn msg : boardmsg =>
       (fn _ : {} =>
         query[] [T : {Channel : FFI(Basis.channel)}] [{}]
          "SELECT T_T.uw_Channel FROM uw_Helloworld_Room_t AS T_T WHERE (T_T.uw_id = "
           ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")" initial {} in
          FFI(Basis.send(r.T.Channel, 
                          (case msg of
                            Highlight a =>
                             "Highlight/" ^
                              FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.X)) ^
                               "/" ^ FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.Y)) | 
                             Position a =>
                              "Position/" ^
                               (urlify_list a.Highlight) ^
                                "/" ^
                                 FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.Id)) ^
                                  "/" ^
                                   FFI(Basis.urlifyBool(a.State.BK))
                                    ^
                                    "/" ^
                                     FFI(Basis.urlifyBool(a.State.BQ))
                                      ^
                                      "/" ^
                                       (case a.State.EnPassant of
                                         None => "None" | 
                                          Some x =>
                                           "Some/" ^
                                            FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(x.X))
                                             ^
                                             "/" ^
                                              FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(x.Y)))
                                        ^
                                        "/" ^
                                         FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.State.FullMove))
                                          ^
                                          "/" ^
                                           FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(a.State.HalfMove))
                                            ^
                                            "/" ^
                                             (urlify_list
                                               a.State.Pieces) ^
                                              "/" ^
                                               (case a.State.Player
                                                 of
                                                 White => "White" | 
                                                  Black => "Black") ^
                                                "/" ^
                                                 FFI(Basis.urlifyBool(a.State.WK))
                                                  ^
                                                  "/" ^
                                                   FFI(Basis.urlifyBool(a.State.WQ))))))))

 datatype
  pgnTree =
   Node of
    {1 : FFI(Basis.int), 2 : FFI(Basis.string), 
      3 : FFI(Basis.string), 4 : FFI(Basis.string), 5 : list(pgnTree)}
 
 datatype
  pgnRoot =
   Root of
    {1 : FFI(Basis.int), 2 : FFI(Basis.string), 3 : list(pgnTree)}
 
 val rec
  $rev'_unpoly as List/rev' :
   list(pgnTree) -> list(pgnTree) -> list(pgnTree) =
   (fn acc : list(pgnTree) =>
     (fn ls : list(pgnTree) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $rev'_unpoly (Some {1 = x, 2 = acc}) ls)))
 
 val rec
  $recurse as Helloworld/recurse :
   option(FFI(Basis.int)) -> FFI(Basis.string) -> {} -> list(pgnTree)
   =
   (fn root : option(FFI(Basis.int)) =>
     (fn fen : FFI(Basis.string) =>
       (fn _ : {} =>
         $rev'_unpoly None
          query[] [Position :
                    {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int), 
                      Move : option(FFI(Basis.string)), 
                      MoveAlg : option(FFI(Basis.string))}] [list(pgnTree)]
           "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_Position.uw_Id, T_Position.uw_Move, T_Position.uw_MoveAlg FROM uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position"
            ^
            (case
              (case root of
                None => "(T_Position.uw_previousPositionId IS NULL)"
                                                                     |
                                                                     
                 Some _ =>
                  (let e2 : FFI(Basis.string) =
                   ((case root of
                      None => "NULL" | 
                       Some y => FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(y)))) in
                   ("((T_Position.uw_previousPositionId = " ^
                     e2 ^
                      ") OR ((T_Position.uw_previousPositionId) IS NULL AND ("
                       ^ e2 ^ ") IS NULL))"))) of
              "1" => "" | where => " WHERE " ^ where) initial None in
           (let v : pgnTree =
            ((case {1 = r.Position.Move, 2 = r.Position.MoveAlg} of
               {1 = Some move, 2 = Some alg} =>
                Node
                 {1 = r.Position.Id, 2 = fen, 3 = move, 4 = alg, 
                   5 =
                    $recurse (Some r.Position.Id) r.Position.Fen {}}
                                                                     |
                                                                     
                {1 = _, 2 = _} =>
                 Node
                  {1 = r.Position.Id, 2 = "", 3 = "", 4 = "", 
                    5 = None})) in (Some {1 = v, 2 = acc})))))
 
 val
  tree3 as Helloworld/tree3 :
   option(FFI(Basis.int)) -> FFI(Basis.string) -> {} -> pgnRoot =
   (fn root : option(FFI(Basis.int)) =>
     (fn parentFen : FFI(Basis.string) =>
       (fn y : {} =>
         (case root of
           None => Root {1 = 0, 2 = "", 3 = None} | 
            Some root' =>
             Root
              {1 = root', 2 = parentFen, 
                3 = $recurse root parentFen {}}))))
 
 val
  tree4 as Helloworld/tree4 : FFI(Basis.int) -> {} -> pgnRoot =
   (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (let current :
        {Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
          Post : {RootPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
        ((case
           query[] [Post : {RootPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
                     Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}] [option({Position
                                                                     :
                                                                     {Fen
                                                                       :
                                                                       FFI(Basis.string)},
                                                                                          
                                                                     Post
                                                                      :
                                                                      {RootPositionId
                                                                        :
                                                                        FFI(Basis.int)}})]
            "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_Post.uw_RootPositionId FROM uw_Helloworld_post AS T_Post JOIN uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position ON (T_Post.uw_rootPositionId = T_Position.uw_id) WHERE (T_Post.uw_id = "
             ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")" initial None in Some r
           of
           None =>
            (error "Query returned no rows" :
             {Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
               Post : {RootPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}) | 
            Some r => r)) in
        (tree3 (Some current.Post.RootPositionId)
          current.Position.Fen {}))))
 
 val
  getRoom as Helloworld/getRoom :
   FFI(Basis.int) -> {} -> FFI(Basis.int) =
   (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (let r : {Post : {Room : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
        ((case
           query[] [Post : {Room : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({Post :
                                                              {Room :
                                                                FFI(Basis.int)}})]
            "SELECT T_Post.uw_Room FROM uw_Helloworld_post AS T_Post WHERE (T_Post.uw_id = "
             ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")" initial None in Some r
           of
           None =>
            (error "Query returned no rows" :
             {Post : {Room : FFI(Basis.int)}}) | Some r => r)) in
        (r.Post.Room))))
 
 val
  speak as Helloworld/speak :
   FFI(Basis.int) -> serverboardmsg -> {} -> {} =
   (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn line : serverboardmsg =>
       (fn y : {} =>
         (case line of
           SMovePiece {1 = src, 2 = dest, 3 = kind} =>
            (let idP : FFI(Basis.int) =
             (nextval("uw_Helloworld_positionSeq")) in
             ((let row :
               {Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
                 Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
               ((case
                  query[] [Post :
                            {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
                            Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}] [option({Position
                                                                            :
                                                                            {Fen
                                                                              :
                                                                              FFI(Basis.string)},
                                                                                                 
                                                                            Post
                                                                             :
                                                                             {CurrentPositionId
                                                                               :
                                                                               FFI(Basis.int)}})]
                   "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_Post.uw_CurrentPositionId FROM uw_Helloworld_post AS T_Post JOIN uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position ON (T_Post.uw_currentPositionId = T_Position.uw_id) WHERE (T_Post.uw_id = "
                    ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")" initial None in
                   Some r of
                  None =>
                   (error "Query returned no rows" :
                    {Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
                      Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}) | 
                   Some r => r)) in
               ((let state :
                 {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
                   EnPassant :
                    option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
                   FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
                   HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
                   Pieces :
                    list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                           Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
                   WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =
                 (fen_to_state row.Position.Fen) in
                 ((case
                    doMove state
                     {Dest = dest, Prom = kind, Src = src} of
                    None => {} | 
                     Some manipulated =>
                      (let newFen : FFI(Basis.string) =
                       (state_to_fen manipulated) in
                       ((let _ : {} =
                         (dml("UPDATE uw_Helloworld_post SET uw_CurrentPositionId = "
                               ^
                               FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^
                                " WHERE (uw_id = " ^
                                 FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")")) in
                         ((let _ : {} =
                           (dml("INSERT INTO uw_Helloworld_position (uw_Fen, uw_Id, uw_Move, uw_MoveAlg, uw_PostId, uw_PreviousPositionId) VALUES ("
                                 ^
                                 FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(newFen)) ^
                                  ", " ^
                                   FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^
                                    ", " ^
                                     FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(moveStr
                                                             {Dest =
                                                               dest, 
                                                               Prom =
                                                                kind, 
                                                               Src =
                                                                src}))
                                      ^
                                      ", " ^
                                       FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(moveToAlgebraicClean
                                                               state
                                                               {Dest
                                                                 =
                                                                 dest,
                                                                      
                                                                 Prom
                                                                  =
                                                                  kind,
                                                                       
                                                                 Src
                                                                  =
                                                                  src}
                                                               manipulated))
                                        ^
                                        ", " ^
                                         FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^
                                          ", " ^
                                           FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(row.Post.CurrentPositionId))
                                            ^ ")")) in
                           (send (getRoom id {})
                             (Position
                               {Highlight = None, Id = idP, 
                                 State = fen_to_state newFen}) {})))))))))))))
                                                                               |
                                                                               
            SBack =>
             (let row : {Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}
              =
              ((case
                 query[] [Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({Post
                                                                                 :
                                                                                 {CurrentPositionId
                                                                                   :
                                                                                   FFI(Basis.int)}})]
                  "SELECT T_Post.uw_CurrentPositionId FROM uw_Helloworld_post AS T_Post WHERE (T_Post.uw_id = "
                   ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")" initial None in
                  Some r of
                 None =>
                  (error "Query returned no rows" :
                   {Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}) | 
                  Some r => r)) in
              ((let row2 :
                {Position :
                  {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
                ((case
                   query[] [Position :
                             {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), 
                               Id : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({Position
                                                               :
                                                               {Fen :
                                                                 FFI(Basis.string),
                                                                                   
                                                                 Id :
                                                                  FFI(Basis.int)}})]
                    "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_Position.uw_Id FROM uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position WHERE ((T_Position.uw_postId = "
                     ^
                     FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^
                      ") AND (T_Position.uw_id < " ^
                       FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(row.Post.CurrentPositionId))
                        ^ ")) ORDER BY T_Position.uw_id DESC LIMIT 1"
                    initial None in Some r of
                   None =>
                    (error "Query returned no rows" :
                     {Position :
                       {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int)}})
                                                                        |
                                                                        
                    Some r => r)) in
                ((let _ : {} =
                  (dml("UPDATE uw_Helloworld_post SET uw_CurrentPositionId = "
                        ^
                        FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(row2.Position.Id)) ^
                         " WHERE (uw_id = " ^
                          FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")")) in
                  (send (getRoom id {})
                    (Position
                      {Highlight = None, Id = row2.Position.Id, 
                        State = fen_to_state row2.Position.Fen}) {}))))))
                                                                          |
                                                                          
            SForward =>
             (let row : {Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}
              =
              ((case
                 query[] [Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({Post
                                                                                 :
                                                                                 {CurrentPositionId
                                                                                   :
                                                                                   FFI(Basis.int)}})]
                  "SELECT T_Post.uw_CurrentPositionId FROM uw_Helloworld_post AS T_Post WHERE (T_Post.uw_id = "
                   ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")" initial None in
                  Some r of
                 None =>
                  (error "Query returned no rows" :
                   {Post : {CurrentPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}) | 
                  Some r => r)) in
              ((let row2 :
                {Position :
                  {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
                ((case
                   query[] [Position :
                             {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), 
                               Id : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({Position
                                                               :
                                                               {Fen :
                                                                 FFI(Basis.string),
                                                                                   
                                                                 Id :
                                                                  FFI(Basis.int)}})]
                    "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_Position.uw_Id FROM uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position WHERE ((T_Position.uw_postId = "
                     ^
                     FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^
                      ") AND (T_Position.uw_id > " ^
                       FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(row.Post.CurrentPositionId))
                        ^ ")) ORDER BY T_Position.uw_id LIMIT 1"
                    initial None in Some r of
                   None =>
                    (error "Query returned no rows" :
                     {Position :
                       {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int)}})
                                                                        |
                                                                        
                    Some r => r)) in
                ((let _ : {} =
                  (dml("UPDATE uw_Helloworld_post SET uw_CurrentPositionId = "
                        ^
                        FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(row2.Position.Id)) ^
                         " WHERE (uw_id = " ^
                          FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")")) in
                  (send (getRoom id {})
                    (Position
                      {Highlight = None, Id = row2.Position.Id, 
                        State = fen_to_state row2.Position.Fen}) {}))))))
                                                                          |
                                                                          
            SPosition idP =>
             (let row2 :
              {Position :
                {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
              ((case
                 query[] [Position :
                           {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), 
                             Id : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({Position
                                                             :
                                                             {Fen :
                                                               FFI(Basis.string),
                                                                                 
                                                               Id :
                                                                FFI(Basis.int)}})]
                  "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_Position.uw_Id FROM uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position WHERE ((T_Position.uw_postId = "
                   ^
                   FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^
                    ") AND (T_Position.uw_id = " ^
                     FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^ "))" initial None in
                  Some r of
                 None =>
                  (error "Query returned no rows" :
                   {Position :
                     {Fen : FFI(Basis.string), Id : FFI(Basis.int)}})
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                  Some r => r)) in
              ((let _ : {} =
                (dml("UPDATE uw_Helloworld_post SET uw_CurrentPositionId = "
                      ^
                      FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^
                       " WHERE (uw_id = " ^
                        FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ")")) in
                (send (getRoom id {})
                  (Position
                    {Highlight = None, Id = idP, 
                      State = fen_to_state row2.Position.Fen}) {}))))
                                                                      |
                                                                      
            SHighlight sq => send (getRoom id {}) (Highlight sq) {}))))
 
 val
  getTree as Helloworld/getTree : FFI(Basis.int) -> {} -> pgnRoot =
   (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) => tree4 id)

 export rpc(r) getTree as Helloworld/getTree (FFI(Basis.int)) ({}) ->
  pgnRoot
 
 val rec
  jsify as jsify : list(pgnTree) -> FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn x : list(pgnTree) =>
     (case x of
       None => "null" | 
        Some x => "{_1:" ^ (jsify x.1) ^ ",_2:" ^ (jsify x.2) ^ "}"))
                                                                      and
                                                                      
   jsify as jsify : pgnTree -> FFI(Basis.string) =
    (fn x : pgnTree =>
      (case x of
        Node x =>
         "{n:4483,v:{_1:" ^
          FFI(Basis.htmlifyInt(x.1)) ^
           ",_2:" ^
            FFI(Basis.jsifyString(x.2)) ^
             ",_3:" ^
              FFI(Basis.jsifyString(x.3)) ^
               ",_4:" ^
                FFI(Basis.jsifyString(x.4)) ^
                 ",_5:" ^ (jsify x.5) ^ "}}"))
 
 val rec
  $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly as List/foldl' :
   FFI(Basis.string) -> list(pgnTree) -> FFI(Basis.string) =
   (fn acc : FFI(Basis.string) =>
     (fn ls : list(pgnTree) =>
       (case ls of
         None => acc | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly
            (acc ^
              " (" ^ ($renderPgnN x None FFIC(Basis.True)) ^ ") ") ls)))
                                                                         and
                                                                         
   $renderPgnN as Helloworld/renderPgnN :
    pgnTree -> list(pgnTree) -> FFI(Basis.bool) -> FFI(Basis.string)
    =
    (fn pgnN : pgnTree =>
      (fn siblings : list(pgnTree) =>
        (fn forceAlg : FFI(Basis.bool) =>
          (case pgnN of
            Node
             {1 = idP, 2 = fen, 3 = move, 4 = moveAlg, 5 = children}
             =>
             (let state :
              {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
                EnPassant :
                 option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
                FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
                Pieces :
                 list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                        Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
                WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =
              (fen_to_state fen) in
              ((case
                 (case forceAlg of
                   FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                    FFIC(Basis.False) => peq White state.Player) of
                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                  FFI(Basis.intToString(state.FullMove)) ^
                   "." ^
                    (case state.Player of Black => ".. " | _ => " ")
                                                                     |
                                                                     
                  FFIC(Basis.False) => "") ^ moveAlg)) ^
              (case siblings of
                None => "" | 
                 Some {1 = _, 2 = _} =>
                  $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly "" siblings) ^
               " " ^
                (case children of
                  None => "" | 
                   Some {1 = a, 2 = siblings'} =>
                    $renderPgnN a siblings'
                     (case siblings of
                       None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                        Some {1 = _, 2 = _} => FFIC(Basis.True)))))))
 
 val rec
  $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly as List/foldl' :
   FFI(Basis.string) -> list(pgnTree) -> {} =
   (fn acc : FFI(Basis.string) =>
     (fn ls : list(pgnTree) =>
       (case ls of
         None => write(acc) | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
           $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly
            (acc ^
              " (" ^ ($renderPgnN x None FFIC(Basis.True)) ^ ") ") ls)))
 
 val rec
  $renderPgnN as Helloworld/renderPgnN :
   pgnTree -> list(pgnTree) -> FFI(Basis.bool) -> {} =
   (fn pgnN : pgnTree =>
     (fn siblings : list(pgnTree) =>
       (fn forceAlg : FFI(Basis.bool) =>
         (case pgnN of
           Node
            {1 = idP, 2 = fen, 3 = move, 4 = moveAlg, 5 = children}
            =>
            ((let state :
              {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
                EnPassant :
                 option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
                FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
                Pieces :
                 list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                        Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
                WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =
              (fen_to_state fen) in
              (((case
                  (case forceAlg of
                    FFIC(Basis.True) => FFIC(Basis.True) | 
                     FFIC(Basis.False) => peq White state.Player) of
                  FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                   (FFI(Basis.htmlifyInt_w(state.FullMove));
                    (write(".");
                     (case state.Player of
                       Black => write(".. ") | _ => write(" ")))) | 
                   FFIC(Basis.False) => {}); write(moveAlg))));
             ((case siblings of
                None => {} | 
                 Some {1 = _, 2 = _} =>
                  $foldl'_unpoly_unpoly "" siblings);
              (write(" ");
               (case children of
                 None => {} | 
                  Some {1 = a, 2 = siblings'} =>
                   $renderPgnN a siblings'
                    (case siblings of
                      None => FFIC(Basis.False) | 
                       Some {1 = _, 2 = _} => FFIC(Basis.True))))))))))
 
 val rec
  $importChildrenAux as Helloworld/importChildrenAux :
   FFI(Basis.int) ->
    FFI(Basis.int) ->
     {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
       EnPassant : option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
       FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
       Pieces :
        list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}),
                                                                      
       Player : player, WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)}
      -> list(pgnTree) -> {} -> {} =
   (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn idP : FFI(Basis.int) =>
       (fn state :
         {BK : FFI(Basis.bool), BQ : FFI(Basis.bool), 
           EnPassant :
            option({X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), 
           FullMove : FFI(Basis.int), HalfMove : FFI(Basis.int), 
           Pieces :
            list({Piece : piece, X : FFI(Basis.int), 
                   Y : FFI(Basis.int)}), Player : player, 
           WK : FFI(Basis.bool), WQ : FFI(Basis.bool)} =>
         (fn children : list(pgnTree) =>
           (fn _ : {} =>
             (case children of
               None => {} | 
                Some {1 = h, 2 = t} =>
                 (case h of
                   Node
                    {1 = _, 2 = _, 3 = move, 4 = _, 5 = children2} =>
                    (let rmove :
                     {Dest : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)},
                                                                      
                       Prom : option(kind), 
                       Src : {X : FFI(Basis.int), Y : FFI(Basis.int)}}
                     = (str_to_move move) in
                     ((case doMove state rmove of
                        None => {} | 
                         Some newState =>
                          (let nidP : FFI(Basis.int) =
                           (nextval("uw_Helloworld_positionSeq")) in
                           ((let nfen : FFI(Basis.string) =
                             (state_to_fen newState) in
                             ((let _ : {} =
                               (dml("INSERT INTO uw_Helloworld_position (uw_Fen, uw_Id, uw_Move, uw_MoveAlg, uw_PostId, uw_PreviousPositionId) VALUES ("
                                     ^
                                     FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(nfen)) ^
                                      ", " ^
                                       FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(nidP)) ^
                                        ", " ^
                                         FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(moveStr
                                                                 rmove))
                                          ^
                                          ", " ^
                                           FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(moveToAlgebraicClean
                                                                   state
                                                                   rmove
                                                                   newState))
                                            ^
                                            ", " ^
                                             FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id))
                                              ^
                                              ", " ^
                                               FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP))
                                                ^ ")")) in
                               ((let _ : {} =
                                 ($importChildren id nidP nfen
                                   children2 {}) in
                                 ($importChildrenAux id idP state t
                                   {}))))))))))))))))))
                                                        and 
   $importChildren as Helloworld/importChildren :
    FFI(Basis.int) ->
     FFI(Basis.int) -> FFI(Basis.string) -> list(pgnTree) -> {} -> {}
    =
    (fn id : FFI(Basis.int) =>
      (fn idP : FFI(Basis.int) =>
        (fn fen : FFI(Basis.string) =>
          (fn children : list(pgnTree) =>
            (fn _ : {} =>
              $importChildrenAux id idP (fen_to_state fen) children
               {})))))
 
 val
  wrap_addPost as Helloworld/addPost :
   {Fil : FFI(Basis.file), Nam : FFI(Basis.string)} -> {} -> {} =
   (fn x0 : {Fil : FFI(Basis.file), Nam : FFI(Basis.string)} =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (case
         (!
           (FFI(Basis.blobSize(FFI(Basis.fileData(x0.Fil)))) <= 10000))
         of
         FFIC(Basis.True) => write("too big") | 
          FFIC(Basis.False) =>
           (let id : FFI(Basis.int) =
            (nextval("uw_Helloworld_postSeq")) in
            ((let idP : FFI(Basis.int) =
              (nextval("uw_Helloworld_positionSeq")) in
              ((let _ : {} =
                (dml("INSERT INTO uw_Helloworld_post (uw_CurrentPositionId, uw_Id, uw_Nam, uw_Room, uw_RootPositionId) VALUES ("
                      ^
                      FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^
                       ", " ^
                        FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^
                         ", " ^
                          FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(x0.Nam)) ^
                           ", " ^
                            FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(nextval("uw_Helloworld_Room_s")))
                             ^ ", " ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^ ")"))
                in
                ((let _ : {} =
                  (dml("INSERT INTO uw_Helloworld_position (uw_Fen, uw_Id, uw_Move, uw_MoveAlg, uw_PostId, uw_PreviousPositionId) VALUES ('rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1', "
                        ^
                        FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(idP)) ^
                         ", NULL, NULL, " ^
                          FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(id)) ^ ", NULL)")) in
                  ((let _ : {} =
                    ($importChildren id idP
                      "rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1"
                      None {}) in
                    (write((redirect "/Helloworld/allPosts" :
                            FFI(Basis.string))))))))))))))))

  Helloworld/addPost
                     ({Fil : FFI(Basis.file), Nam : FFI(Basis.string)})
                      ({}) -> {}
 
 val
  wrap_createPost as Helloworld/createPost : {} -> {} -> {} =

     (fn _ : {} =>
       (write("\n<body");
        (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onload(FFI(Basis.get_settings({})))));
         (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onunload("")));
          write(">\n<form method=\"post\" action=\"/Helloworld/addPost\" enctype=\"multipart/form-data\">\n<table>\t<tr><th>Name:</th><td><input type=\"text\" name=\"Nam\" /></td></tr>\n<tr><th>File (optional):</th><td><input type=\"file\" name=\"Fil\" /></td></tr>\n<tr><th></th><td><input type=\"submit\" value=\"Create\" /></td></tr>\n</table>\n</form>\n</body>\n"))))))
 
 val
  wrap_postPage as Helloworld/postPage :
   FFI(Basis.int) -> {} -> {} -> {} =
   (fn x1 : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn x0 : {} =>
       (fn _ : {} =>
         (let current :
          {Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
            PositionR : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
            Post :
             {Nam : FFI(Basis.string), Room : FFI(Basis.int), 
               RootPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}} =
          ((case
             query[] [Post :
                       {Nam : FFI(Basis.string), 
                         Room : FFI(Basis.int), 
                         RootPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}, 
                       Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
                       PositionR : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}] [option({Position
                                                                        :
                                                                        {Fen
                                                                          :
                                                                          FFI(Basis.string)},
                                                                                             
                                                                        PositionR
                                                                         :
                                                                         {Fen
                                                                           :
                                                                           FFI(Basis.string)},
                                                                                              
                                                                        Post
                                                                         :
                                                                         {Nam
                                                                           :
                                                                           FFI(Basis.string),
                                                                                             
                                                                           Room
                                                                            :
                                                                            FFI(Basis.int),
                                                                                           
                                                                           RootPositionId
                                                                            :
                                                                            FFI(Basis.int)}})]
              "SELECT T_Position.uw_Fen, T_PositionR.uw_Fen, T_Post.uw_Nam, T_Post.uw_Room, T_Post.uw_RootPositionId FROM uw_Helloworld_post AS T_Post JOIN uw_Helloworld_position AS T_Position ON (T_Post.uw_currentPositionId = T_Position.uw_id) JOIN uw_Helloworld_position AS T_PositionR ON (T_Post.uw_rootPositionId = T_PositionR.uw_id) WHERE (T_Post.uw_id = "
               ^ FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(x1)) ^ ")" initial None in
              Some r of
             None =>
              (error "Query returned no rows" :
               {Position : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
                 PositionR : {Fen : FFI(Basis.string)}, 
                 Post :
                  {Nam : FFI(Basis.string), Room : FFI(Basis.int), 
                    RootPositionId : FFI(Basis.int)}}) | Some r => r))
          in
          ((let pgnstate : source =
            (FFI(Basis.new_client_source("{c:\"c\",v:" ^
                                          (case
                                            tree3
                                             (Some
                                               current.Post.RootPositionId)
                                             current.PositionR.Fen {}
                                            of
                                            Root x =>
                                             "{n:4485,v:{_1:" ^
                                              FFI(Basis.htmlifyInt(x.1))
                                               ^

 val
  main as Helloworld/main : {} -> {} -> {} =
   (fn $x : {} =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (let u :
        option({Id : FFI(Basis.int), Nam : FFI(Basis.string)}) =
        ((case unurlify(FFI(Basis.get_cookie("Helloworld/login"))) of
           None => None | 
            Some r =>
             (let row :
              {User : {Id : FFI(Basis.int), Nam : FFI(Basis.string)}}
              =
              ((case
                 query[] [User :
                           {Id : FFI(Basis.int), 
                             Nam : FFI(Basis.string)}] [option({User
                                                                 :
                                                                 {Id
                                                                   :
                                                                   FFI(Basis.int),
                                                                                  
                                                                   Nam
                                                                    :
                                                                    FFI(Basis.string)}})]
                  "SELECT T_User.uw_Id, T_User.uw_Nam FROM uw_Helloworld_user AS T_User WHERE ((T_User.uw_id = "
                   ^
                   FFI(Basis.sqlifyInt(r.Id)) ^
                    ") AND (T_User.uw_pass = " ^
                     FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(r.Pass)) ^ "))" initial
                  None in Some r of
                 None =>
                  (error "Query returned no rows" :
                   {User :
                     {Id : FFI(Basis.int), Nam : FFI(Basis.string)}})
                                                                      |
                                                                      
                  Some r => r)) in (Some row.User)))) in
        ((case u of
           None =>
            (write("\n<body");
             (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onload(FFI(Basis.get_settings({})))));
              (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onunload("")));
               write(">\n<form method=\"post\" action=\"/Helloworld/logon\">\n<table>\n<tr><th>Name</th><td><input type=\"text\" name=\"Nam\" /></td></tr>\n<tr><th>Password:</th><td><input type=\"text\" name=\"Pass\" /></td></tr>\n<tr><td><input type=\"submit\" /></td></tr>\n<tr></tr>\n</table>\n</form>\n</body>\n"))))
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
            Some u =>
             (write("\n<body");
              (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onload(FFI(Basis.get_settings({})))));
               (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onunload("")));
                (write(">\n<h1>Welcome to the turtle corner! ");
                 (FFI(Basis.htmlifyString_w(u.Nam));
                  write("</h1>\n<a href=\"/Helloworld/index\">index</a>\n</body>\n")))))))))))
 
 val
  wrap_main as Helloworld/main : {} -> {} -> {} =
   (fn x0 : {} => (fn _ : {} => main x0 {}))
 
 val
  wrap_logon as Helloworld/logon :
   {Nam : FFI(Basis.string), Pass : FFI(Basis.string)} -> {} -> {} =
   (fn x0 : {Nam : FFI(Basis.string), Pass : FFI(Basis.string)} =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (case
         query[] [User : {Id : FFI(Basis.int)}] [option({User :
                                                          {Id :
                                                            FFI(Basis.int)}})]
          "SELECT T_User.uw_Id FROM uw_Helloworld_user AS T_User WHERE ((T_User.uw_nam = "
           ^
           FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(x0.Nam)) ^
            ") AND (T_User.uw_pass = " ^
             FFI(Basis.sqlifyString(x0.Pass)) ^ "))" initial None in
          Some r of
         None =>
          write((error "Wrong user or pass!" : FFI(Basis.string))) | 
          Some r' =>
           (let _ : {} =
            (FFI(Basis.set_cookie("/", "Helloworld/login", 
                                   FFI(Basis.urlifyInt(r'.User.Id)) ^
                                    "/" ^
                                     FFI(Basis.urlifyString(x0.Pass)),
                                                                      
                                   None, FFIC(Basis.False)))) in
            (main {} {})))))

 val rec
  $nth_unpoly as List/nth :
   list(FFI(Basis.string)) ->
    FFI(Basis.int) -> option(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn ls : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
     (fn n : FFI(Basis.int) =>
       (case ls of
         None => None | 
          Some {1 = x, 2 = ls'} =>
           (case (n <= 0) of
             FFIC(Basis.True) => Some x | 
              FFIC(Basis.False) => $nth_unpoly ls' (n - 1)))))
 
 val rec
  $mp'_unpoly_unpoly as List/mp' :
   FFI(Basis.string) ->
    list(FFI(Basis.string)) ->
     list({Len : FFI(Basis.int), Start : FFI(Basis.int)}) ->
      list(FFI(Basis.string)) =
   (fn l : FFI(Basis.string) =>
     (fn acc : list(FFI(Basis.string)) =>
       (fn ls : list({Len : FFI(Basis.int), Start : FFI(Basis.int)})
         =>
         (case ls of
           None => $rev'_unpoly None acc | 
            Some {1 = x, 2 = ls} =>
             $mp'_unpoly_unpoly l (Some {1 = substring l x, 2 = acc})
              ls))))

                       FFI(Basis.strsuffix("[Event \"Reykjavik Open\"]\n[Site \"Reykjavik, Iceland\"]\n[Date \"????.??.??\"]\n[Round \"8.1\"]\n[White \"Adhiban, Baskaran\"]\n[Black \"Rapport, Richard\"]\n[Result \"1-0\"]\n[ECO \"D15\"]\n[PlyCount \"54\"]\n\n1. d4 {[%emt 0:00:27]} d5 {[%emt 0:01:11]} 2. c4 {[%emt 0:00:42]} c6 {[%emt 0:\n00:06]} 3. Nf3 {[%emt 0:02:33]} Nf6 {[%emt 0:00:30]} 4. Nc3 {[%emt 0:00:05]}\ndxc4 {[%emt 0:00:05]} 5. e4 {[%emt 0:02:39]} b5 {[%emt 0:00:26]} 6. Be2 {\n[%emt 0:00:01]} e6 {[%emt 0:01:31]} 7. O-O {[%emt 0:00:46]} Be7 {[%emt 0:03:04]\n} 8. a4 {[%emt 0:03:34]} b4 {[%emt 0:00:44]} 9. e5 {[%emt 0:00:08]} bxc3 {\n[%emt 0:02:06]} 10. exf6 {[%emt 0:00:05]} Bxf6 {[%emt 0:00:14]} 11. bxc3 {\n[%emt 0:00:07]} Ba6 {[%emt 0:00:37]} 12. Ne5 {[%emt 0:17:30]} Bxe5 {[%emt 0:04:\n41]} 13. dxe5 {[%emt 0:00:02]} Qxd1 {[%emt 0:00:25]} 14. Rxd1 {[%emt 0:00:02]}\nNd7 {[%emt 0:00:07]} 15. f4 {[%emt 0:04:04]} Nb6 {[%emt 0:04:54]} 16. Rd6 {\n[%emt 0:02:24]} O-O {[%emt 0:13:59]} 17. Bf3 {[%emt 0:08:12]} Nc8 {[%emt 0:07:\n22]} 18. Rxc6 {[%emt 0:02:30]} Bb7 {[%emt 0:00:29]} 19. Rxc8 {[%emt 0:00:02]}\nRaxc8 {[%emt 0:00:05]} 20. Bxb7 {[%emt 0:00:05]} Rb8 {[%emt 0:00:12]} 21. Ba6 {\n[%emt 0:02:05]} Rb3 {[%emt 0:00:15]} 22. Ba3 {[%emt 0:00:48]} Rd8 {[%emt 0:00:\n11]} 23. Bb4 {[%emt 0:00:47]} Rd2 {[%emt 0:00:39]} 24. Bxc4 {[%emt 0:00:11]}\nRbb2 {[%emt 0:00:02]} 25. Bf1 {[%emt 0:00:30]} h5 {[%emt 0:00:10]} 26. a5 {\n[%emt 0:02:24]} a6 {[%emt 0:00:16]} 27. Bc5 {[%emt 0:03:33]} g6 {[%emt 0:00:52]\n} 1-0\n",
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
                                            (i +
                                              FFI(Basis.strlen("\n")))))})
               of
               None => None | 
                Some {1 = l, 2 = rest} =>
                 (case
                   (case
                     (let substrings :
                      FFI(Regex__FFI.substring_list_t) =
                      (FFI(Regex__FFI.do_match((case
                                                 FFI(Basis.strlenGe("Event ",
                                                                             
                                                                     1))
                                                 of
                                                 FFIC(Basis.True) =>
                                                  "Event " | 
                                                  FFIC(Basis.False)
                                                   =>
                                                   (error
                                                    "regex: Empty regex"
                                                    :
                                                    FFI(Basis.string))),
                                                                        
                                                l))) in
                      ((case
                         FFI(Regex__FFI.substring_list_length(substrings))
                         of
                         0 => None | 
                          n_groups =>
                           Some
                            {Groups = $loop substrings n_groups 1, 
                              Whole =
                               unmarshal_substring
                                FFI(Regex__FFI.substring_list_get(substrings,
                                                                             
                                                                   0))})))
                     of
                     None => None | 
                      Some y =>
                       Some
                        {Groups = $mp'_unpoly_unpoly l None y.Groups, 
                          Whole = substring l y.Whole}) of
                   None => None | 
                    Some m =>
                     (case $nth_unpoly m.Groups 0 of
                       None => None | Some v => Some {1 = v, 2 = ""})))
             of
             None => "none" | 
              Some {1 = s1, 2 = s2} =>
               "\n<div>head: " ^
                FFI(Basis.htmlifyString(s1)) ^
                 "</div>\n<div>rest: " ^
                  FFI(Basis.htmlifyString(s2)) ^ "</div>\n") ^
            "\n</body>\n") in ((fn _ : {} => write(x)))))
 
 val
  wrap_testResponsive as Helloworld/testResponsive : {} -> {} -> {} =
   (fn x0 : {} =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (write("\n<head>\n<link href=\"/bootstrap.min.css\" rel=\"stylesheet\" type=\"text/css\" />\n</head>\n<body");
        (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onload(FFI(Basis.get_settings({})))));
         (write(FFI(Basis.maybe_onunload("")));
          write(">\n<div class=\"container\">\n<div class=\"row\"> </div>\n</div>\n</body>\n"))))))
 
 val
  wrap_downloadPost as Helloworld/downloadPost :
   FFI(Basis.int) -> {} -> {} =
   (fn x0 : FFI(Basis.int) =>
     (fn _ : {} =>
       (let tree : pgnRoot = (tree4 x0 {}) in
        ((let _ : {} =
          (FFI(Basis.setHeader("Content-Disposition", 
                                "attachment; filename=post_" ^
                                 FFI(Basis.intToString(x0)) ^ ".pgn")))
          in
          (write((FFI(Basis.clear_page());
                  ((case tree of
                     Root {1 = _, 2 = _, 3 = None} => write("*") | 
                      Root
                       {1 = _, 2 = _, 3 = Some {1 = a, 2 = siblings}}
                       => $renderPgnN a siblings FFIC(Basis.False));
                   (blob <page> in "application/octet-stream" :
                    FFI(Basis.string)))))))))))

  {}

  Helloworld/downloadPost (FFI(Basis.int)) ({}) -> {}
